il_cc1=\"19\" il_cc2=\"19\"><p data-iceapw=\"116\">When you talk about the search engine priority for a blog, HTTPS plays an important role to drive organic traffic for your blog or site. We all know that HTTPS-enabled sites are more secure than HTTP-enabled sites. HTTPS sites use Secure Socket Layer (SSL) concept to protect sites data during connections between web server and client. Typically, you need to pay something to use SSL certificate and convert your HTTP site to HTTPS. However, almost all the web hosting services provides a free SSL certificates with limited features that we can use to enhance the security and reliability of our blogs and sites. Here, we will discuss how to activate free WordPress SSL certificate for <a href=\"https://www.bluehost.com/track/protechgurus/\">BlueHost </a>domain.</p><p data-iceapw=\"16\" class=\" IL_IC_MIN\">To Activate Free WordPress SSL Certificate for BlueHost domain, you need to follow the following instructions.<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"IL_IN_ARTICLE\" value=\"1\" class=\"IL_IN_AUTO\"><div class=\"IL_BASE\" style=\"margin: 5px auto; height: 0px; text-align: center; display: inline-block; padding: 0px; overflow: hidden;\"><div class=\"IL_BASE\" style=\"border-style: solid; border-width: 1.33333px; border-color: rgb(202, 202, 202); position: relative; margin: 0px auto; width: 693px; height: 100px; transform: scale(1); transform-origin: 0px 0px 0px; perspective: 1000px; cursor: pointer;\"><div data-il_in_article0_2_0_mtuxfnd3dy5zdxblcnbhz2vzlmnvbq=\"\" style=\"display: none\"></div>                                <!--<div id=\"IL_IN_ARTICLE_LOGO_0\" class=\"IL_BASE IL_LOGO\" style=\"z-index: 1000; bottom:0; right:0;position: absolute; cursor:pointer;\">                <?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"utf-8\"?>                <!-- Generator: Adobe Illustrator 18.1.1, SVG Export Plug-In . privacy, login to your BlueHost account and navigate to the Domain section. Click on the &nbsp;Domains tab, select your domain name, and then select the Privacy tab as shown in the following figure.</p><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img If you not disable domain privacy, you will get an email from <a href=\"https://www.bluehost.com/track/protechgurus/\">BlueHost</a> and then you need to validate your action. That is an extra activity hence we choose to disable domain privacy temporary. Once the Free SSL certificate is implemented, just enable this feature back again.</p><h3>Installing Free SSL Certificate</h3><p data-iceapw=\"52\" data-iceapc=\"2\">After disabling domain privacy, you can proceed to actual task that is “Turning on Free SSL Certificate” for your WordPress blog. To do so, click the <strong data-iceapw=\"2\">WordPress Tools</strong> option, select <strong data-iceapw=\"1\">Security</strong> in the left pane, and then click slide the Turn On Free SSL Certificate button as shown in the following figure.</p><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" Keep refreshing your page to check the process has finished or not.</p></blockquote><h3>Redirecting HTTP Traffic to HTTPS in WordPress</h3><p data-iceapw=\"42\" data-iceapc=\"3\">Once the SSL certificate installation is done, you need to update the .htaccess file to redirect all the HTTP traffic to HTTPS URLs. To do so, scroll-down to <strong data-iceapw=\"1\">Files</strong>&nbsp;section and then click the <strong data-iceapw=\"2\">File Manager</strong> as shown in the following figure.<img the file and close the <strong data-iceapw=\"2\">File Manager</strong>.</p><h3>Installing Really Simple SSL Plugin.</h3><p data-iceapw=\"40\" data-iceapc=\"1\">The Really Simple SSL plugin automatically detects your settings and configure your website to run over HTTPS. Installation of this plugin is pretty simple, just <span id=\"IL_AD6\" class=\"IL_AD\">install</span> and activate it. Finally, you need to click <strong data-iceapw=\"4\">Go ahead, activate SSL!</strong> button to proceed.</p><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple.png\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-2237\" alt=\"Install Really Simple SSL\" width=\"571\" height=\"445\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple.png 571w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-300x234.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-100x78.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-150x117.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-200x156.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-450x351.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 571px) 100vw, 571px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-2237\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple.png\" alt=\"Install Really Simple SSL\" width=\"571\" height=\"445\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple.png 571w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-300x234.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-100x78.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-150x117.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-200x156.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ssl-really-simple-450x351.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 571px) 100vw, 571px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><p data-iceapw=\"69\" data-iceapc=\"2\">Now your website is ready to be served with HTTPS traffic. However, here one more thing is still pending. If your website has internal linking (that should be) with HTTP URLs, it is recommended to replace all those with HTTPS. To simplify it, you may use the <strong data-iceapw=\"3\">Better Search Replace</strong> plugin, just install it and open it by clicking Tools. Follow the instructions as mentioned in the following figure.<img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2240\" alt=\"\" width=\"649\" height=\"618\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace.png 755w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-600x571.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-300x286.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-100x95.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-150x143.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-200x190.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-450x429.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 649px) 100vw, 649px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2240\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"649\" height=\"618\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace.png 755w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-600x571.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-300x286.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-100x95.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-150x143.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-200x190.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/better-search-replace-450x429.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 649px) 100vw, 649px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><p data-iceapw=\"55\">Save the settings you made with Search and Replace plugin. That’s all you need to install and activate Free SSL Certificate for your <a href=\"https://www.bluehost.com/track/protechgurus/\">BlueHost </a>domain. HTTPS-enabled sites are more secure, reliable, and trusty for the users as well as for the search engines. Hope, you have enjoyed this post. il_cc2=\"18\"><p data-iceapw=\"83\">There are many small bloggers who want to earn money through monetizing his/her blog. Since, no other monetizing platform is better than Google Adsense, but Google Adsense has pretty difficult process and requirements to get the approval. There are many other Google Adsense alternatives that bloggers can use to monetize his/her blog, but Infolinks is one of simplest and best alternative for Google Adsense, at least in my opinion. Here, we would explain the <span id=\"IL_AD5\" class=\"IL_AD\">step by step</span> process “how to apply Infolinks request and getting approved.</p><p data-iceapw=\"61\">Infolinks is my one of the most loved blog monetize platform due to its simplicity of getting approval. Infolinks is also pretty reliable in term of getting paid. However, Infolinks does not pay as much as you may be paid by Google Adsense. Still, Infolinks is the best monetize platform for small bloggers who did not get approval from Google Adsense.</p><p data-iceapw=\"15\">In order to apply Infolinks and getting approval, you need to follow the following steps.</p><h3>Sign Up For Infolinks</h3><p data-iceapw=\"29\"><a href=\"http://www.infolinks.com/join-us?aid=2852060\">Signing up for Infolinks</a> is very simple and it requires just a few minutes to create Infolinks account. To Sign Up for the Infolinks, just click the following Infolinks official <span id=\"IL_AD4\" class=\"IL_AD\">website link</span> to get started.</p><p><a href=\"http://www.infolinks.com/join-us?aid=2852060\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/sign-up-form-450x213.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 611px) 100vw, 611px\" /&gt;</noscript></a></p><p data-iceapw=\"22\" data-iceapc=\"1\">In the next, step, you need to fill the required information in the sign up form as soon in the following figure.<img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/infolinks-sign-up1-300x333.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/infolinks-sign-up1-100x111.png 100w, il_cc1=\"1\" il_cc2=\"1\"><p data-iceapw=\"12\">Do not use any of the fake information during the signing up.</p></blockquote><p data-iceapw=\"45\">Once you are signed up for Infolinks, the Infolinks support team will review your website and other information. Once they found your blog eligible as per their policies, which is most likely in most of the time, you will get a welcome mail from them.</p><h3>Integrating Infolinks with WordPress</h3><p data-iceapw=\"77\">Once your request is approved, which may take 2-3 days, sign in to your Infolinks. Since, there are various platforms on which you can host your blog but I personally found WordPress as most helpful and easier to use than others. We assume that your blog is hosted on WordPress. In order to integrate Infolinks with your blog, their is dedicated WordPress plugin for Infolinks is available that makes it easier to integrate Infolinks with WordPress blog.</p><p data-iceapw=\"40\" data-iceapc=\"3\">In the Infolinks account console, click on the <strong data-iceapw=\"1\">Integrate</strong> tab&nbsp;and then select your blog platform such as <strong data-iceapw=\"1\">WordPress</strong> as soon in the following figure. <span id=\"IL_AD2\" class=\"IL_AD\">Download</span> the Infolinks setup file as it will be used later during installation of Infolinks Plugin.<img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/integrate-infolinks2.png\" sizes=\"(max-width: 624px) 100vw, 624px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><h3>Installing Infolinks WordPress Plugin.</h3><p data-iceapw=\"48\">In the next step, you need to install Infolinks WordPress plugin that you have <span id=\"IL_AD3\" class=\"IL_AD\">downloaded</span> in the previous step or you can directly search it in WordPress plugin directory. The installation of Infolinks WordPress plugin is pretty simple and should not be a challenge for even the new bloggers.</p><h3>Activating Infolinks Plugin</h3><p data-iceapw=\"28\" data-iceapc=\"1\">In this step, you need to activate and validate the Infolinks plugin with your blog. sizes=\"(max-width: 498px) 100vw, 498px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><p data-iceapw=\"15\">That’s all you need to do to apply Infolinks and integrate it with WordPress blog.</p><h3>Customizing Infolinks Ads Display</h3><p data-iceapw=\"42\" data-iceapc=\"1\">Once your Infolinks request is approved and you are done with integration, next you need to customize and adjust the Ads display settings. After 2-3 months, my earning crossed more than $50 per month with Infolinks. So please keep patience and focus on increasing organic traffic for your blog. It is good earning assuming that I am also a new blogger very much like you.</p></blockquote><h3>Getting Paid by Infolinks</h3><p data-iceapw=\"36\" data-iceapc=\"1\">Infolinks pay you your money once it reaches to $50. href=\"https://protechgurus.com/category/blogging-tutorilas/\">Blogging Tutorilas</a></div><div class=\"post-edit\"></div></div><div id=\"post-2198\" class=\"post-2198 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-protechgurus\" data-iceapw=\"517\" data-iceapc=\"42\"><h2 class=\"entry-title post-title\"><a href=\"https://protechgurus.com/install-mongodb-linux-ubuntu-steps/\" rel=\"bookmark\">How To Install MongoDB on Linux (Ubuntu) – Step By Step Guide</a></h2><div class=\"post-meta\" data-iceapw=\"4\" data-iceapc=\"5\">\n<span class=\"meta-prep meta-prep-author posted\" data-iceapw=\"2\">Posted on </span><a href=\"https://protechgurus.com/install-mongodb-linux-ubuntu-steps/\" title=\"How To Install MongoDB on Linux (Ubuntu) – Step By Step Guide\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"timestamp updated\" datetime=\"2017-04-02T14:07:10+00:00\">April 2, 2017</time></a><span class=\"byline\" data-iceapw=\"1\"> by </span><span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://protechgurus.com/author/kamalitexpert/\" title=\"View all posts by ProTechGurus\"><span class=\"author-gravtar\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c81e22ee108c67fa3cd569aae2c15a4a?s=32&amp;d=wavatar&amp;r=g\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c81e22ee108c67fa3cd569aae2c15a4a?s=64&amp;d=wavatar&amp;r=g 2x\" class=\"avatar avatar-32 photo\" height=\"32\" width=\"32\"><noscript>&lt;img\nalt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c81e22ee108c67fa3cd569aae2c15a4a?s=32&amp;#038;d=wavatar&amp;#038;r=g' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c81e22ee108c67fa3cd569aae2c15a4a?s=64&amp;amp;d=wavatar&amp;amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-32 photo' height='32' width='32' /&gt;</noscript></span>ProTechGurus</a></span>\n<span class=\"comments-link\" data-iceapw=\"1\" data-iceapc=\"1\">\n<span class=\"mdash\" data-iceapw=\"1\">—</span>\n<a href=\"https://protechgurus.com/install-mongodb-linux-ubuntu-steps/#respond\">No Comments ↓</a>\t\t</span></div><div class=\"post-entry\" data-iceapw=\"511\" data-iceapc=\"33\" il_cc1=\"17\" il_cc2=\"17\"><p data-iceapw=\"129\">In nowadays, MongoDB getting to much popularity among the developers and database administrators. Unlike MySQL, MongoDB is a NoSQL database. It offers various rich features such as high performance, high availability, and automatic scaling enterprise database. &nbsp;Since MongoDB is a NoSQL database, so you cannot use Structured Query Language to insert and retrieve data. In addition, unlike MySQL or Postgres, it does not store data in form of tables. With MongoDB, the data is stored in a “document” structure using special format called JSON. When it comes to open source, nothing is much preferred than using a Linux variants. The most popular Linux variant used by open source developers is Ubuntu. Here, we are going to discuss the step by step guide how to install MongoDB on Ubuntu Linux.</p><h2>Installing MongoDB on Ubuntu/Linux</h2><p data-iceapw=\"15\">In order to install MongoDB on Ubuntu Linux, you need to perform the following steps:</p><h3>1. Importing the Public Key</h3><p data-iceapw=\"43\">GPG keys are used to ensure consistency and authenticity of the packages you want to install. It is always recommended to use only authorized packages. In order to import hte GPG keys for MongoDb package, execute the following command on a Ubuntu machine:</p><pre data-iceapw=\"7\">sudo apt-key adv --keyserver hkp://keyserver.ubuntu.com:80 --recv EA312927</pre><h3>2. Creating Source List File for MongoDB</h3><p data-iceapw=\"24\">After adding the GPG key, next create a MongoDB list file under the /etc/apt/sources.list.d/ directory. For this, you need to execute the following command:</p><pre data-iceapw=\"10\">echo \"deb http://repo.mongodb.org/apt/ubuntu \"$(lsb_release -sc)\"/mongodb-org/3.2 multiverse\" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/mongodb-org-3.2.list</pre><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2202 size-full\" title=\"Install MongoDB Linux\" alt=\"Install MongoDB on Linux\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2202 size-full\" title=\"Install MongoDB Linux\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20.png\" alt=\"Install MongoDB on Linux\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_12h58_20-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><h3>3. Installing the MongoDB Packages</h3><p data-iceapw=\"20\">Now, you are ready to install the MongoDB packages. To install the MongoDB on Ubuntu server, execute the following commands:</p><pre data-iceapw=\"8\">sudo apt-get update\nsudo apt-get install -y mongodb-org</pre><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2203 size-full\" alt=\"Installing MongoDB Linux\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2203 size-full\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28.png\" alt=\"Installing MongoDB Linux\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h00_28-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><h3>4. Creating MongoDB Service Script File</h3><p data-iceapw=\"56\" data-iceapc=\"2\">Once the MongoDB packages are installed, you can start the <strong data-iceapw=\"1\">MongoDB</strong> service. However, in the latest version of Ubuntu such as <strong data-iceapw=\"2\">Ubuntu 16.04</strong>, you may get an daemon error. To avoid this, you need to create a new mongodb systemd service file under the “/lib/systemd/system” directory. For this, you need to execute the following command:</p><pre data-iceapw=\"3\">sudo vim /lib/systemd/system/mongod.service.</pre><p data-iceapw=\"18\">The above command will open a new file in which you need to insert the following script carefully.</p><pre data-iceapw=\"16\">[Unit]\nDescription=High-performance, schema-free document-oriented database\nAfter=network.target\nDocumentation=https://docs.mongodb.org/manual\n\n[Service]\nUser=mongodb\nGroup=mongodb\nExecStart=/usr/bin/mongod --quiet --config /etc/mongod.conf\n\n[Install]\nWantedBy=multi-user.target</pre><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2204 size-full\" alt=\"Starting MongoDB Service on Ubuntu 16.04 error\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2204 size-full\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03.png\" alt=\"Starting MongoDB Service on Ubuntu 16.04 error\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h03_03-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><h3>5. Starting and Enabling MongoDB Service</h3><p data-iceapw=\"15\">In the next step, you need to update the systemd services using the following command:</p><pre data-iceapw=\"3\">sudo systemctl daemon-reload</pre><p data-iceapw=\"27\">Now you are ready to start the MongoDB service. Use the following commands to start the MongoDB server and enable it for starting at each boot time.</p><pre data-iceapw=\"8\">sudo systemctl start mongod\nsudo systemctl enable mongod</pre><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2205 size-full\" alt=\"Starting MongoDB service\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2205 size-full\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14.png\" alt=\"Starting MongoDB service\" width=\"700\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14.png 700w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-600x282.png 600w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-300x141.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-100x47.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-150x71.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-200x94.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h04_14-450x212.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><h3>6. Verifying MongoDB Ports</h3><p data-iceapw=\"33\">In the above figure, you can see the MongoDB service is started and running fine. Here you can also check whether the MongoDB has been started on port 27017 with the netstat command.</p><pre data-iceapw=\"3\">sudo netstat -plntu</pre><h3>7. Connecting MongoDB Terminal</h3><p data-iceapw=\"39\">Once the installation is done, you can connect to MongoDB terminal and execute the commands for the tasks you want to do. In the following figure, you can see the MongoDB terminal is connected and ready to be used.</p><pre data-iceapw=\"2\">sudo mongo</pre><p data-iceapc=\"1\"><img src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif\" data-lazy-src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20.png\" class=\"aligncenter wp-image-2206 size-full\" alt=\"Connecting MongoDB Terminal\" width=\"595\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20.png 595w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-300x166.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-100x55.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-150x83.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-200x111.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-450x249.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 595px) 100vw, 595px\"><noscript>&lt;img\nclass=\"aligncenter wp-image-2206 size-full\" src=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20.png\" alt=\"Connecting MongoDB Terminal\" width=\"595\" height=\"329\" srcset=\"https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20.png 595w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-300x166.png 300w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-100x55.png 100w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-150x83.png 150w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-200x111.png 200w, https://protechgurus.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/2017-04-02_13h49_20-450x249.png 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 595px) 100vw, 595px\" /&gt;</noscript></p><p data-iceapw=\"32\">In this post, we have explained how to install MongoDB on Ubuntu Linux machine. Hope, you have enjoyed it. If you face any issue or have any query, please let us know.</p></div><div class=\"post-data\" data-iceapw=\"2\">\nPosted in <a
